Details of amounts\nowed to group companies are shown in Note 7.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:&#xD;&#xA;9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><b><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">DIVIDENDS AND RESERVES</span></b><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:&#xD;&#xA;9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">The profit and loss account for the year\nended 31 December 2011 is set out on page </span><span style=\"font-size:&#xD;&#xA;11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-no-proof:&#xD;&#xA;yes\">6</span></span><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><a></a>. &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black;background:white;mso-highlight:white\">Company\n law requires the directors to prepare financial statements for each financial\n year.<a></a> Under that law the directors have elected to prepare\n the financial statements in accordance<a></a> with United Kingdom\n Generally Accepted Accounting Practice (United Kingdom Accounting<a></a> Standards and applicable law). Under company law the\n directors must not approve the<a></a> financial statements unless\n they are satisfied that they give a true and fair view of the state of affairs\n of the company and of the profit or loss of the company for that period.<a></a> In preparing these financial statements, the directors are\n required to:</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA; </span>Those standards require us\nto comply with the Auditing<a></a> Practices Board's Ethical\nStandards for Auditors.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" statements\nsufficient to give reasonable assurance that the financial statements are free<a></a> from material misstatement, whether caused by fraud or error.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>This includes an assessment<a></a>\nof: whether the accounting policies are appropriate to the company's\ncircumstances and have<a></a> been consistently applied and\nadequately disclosed; the reasonableness of significant<a></a>\naccounting estimates made by the directors; and the overall presentation of the\nfinancial<a></a> statements.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\"> \n</span>In addition, we read all the financial and non-financial information in\nthe<a></a> annual report to identify material inconsistencies with\nthe audited financial statements. If we become aware of any apparent material\nmisstatements or inconsistencies we consider<a></a> the\nimplications for our report.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" to the profit and loss account in\nthe period in which the rents become due.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" periods, are received upon entering into\nthe lease, the benefit is recognised as an adjustment to rents payable allocated\nevenly over the lease term or the term to the first open market rent review if\nearlier.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Finance lease agreements</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:&#xD;&#xA;-23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Amounts\ndue from lessees under finance leases are recognised as receivables at the net\ninvestment in the leases.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>Finance lease\nincome is allocated to accounting periods so as to reflect a constant periodic\nrate of return on the net investment outstanding in respect of the lease.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:&#xD;&#xA;23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Trade and other debtors</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:&#xD;&#xA;-23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Debtors\nare recognised initially at fair value.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\"> \n</span>A provision for impairment is established where there is objective\nevidence that the company will not be able to collect all amounts due according\nto the original terms of the debtor concerned.</span></p></div><div><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-ansi-language:EN-GB;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-language:EN-GB;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA\"><br /></span></div><div class=\"WordSection11\"><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:&#xD;&#xA;23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Debt</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:&#xD;&#xA;-23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Debt\ninstruments are stated initially at the amount of the net proceeds. The finance\ncosts of such debt instruments are allocated to periods over the term of the\ndebt at a constant rate on the carrying amount. The carrying amount is\nincreased by the finance cost in respect of the reporting period and reduced by\npayments made in respect of the debt of that period. Finance costs are charged\nto the profit and loss account.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:&#xD;&#xA;23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Taxation</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:&#xD;&#xA;-23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Current\ntax is provided at amounts expected to be paid or recovered using the tax rates\nand laws that have been enacted or substantively enacted at the balance sheet\ndate. The company is part of a UK group for group relief purposes and\naccordingly may take advantage of the group relief provisions whereby current\ntaxable profits can be offset by current tax losses arising in other companies\nin that group.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>The group's policy is\nthat no payment will be made for tax losses surrendered under the group relief\nprovisions.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:&#xD;&#xA;-23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Deferred\ntax assets and liabilities arise from timing differences between the\nrecognition of gains and losses in the financial statements and their\nrecognition in the corporation tax return.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:&#xD;&#xA;-23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Under\nFRS 19 deferred tax is recognised in respect of all timing differences that\nhave originated but not reversed at the balance sheet date where transactions\nor events that result in an obligation to pay more tax in the future or a right\nto pay less tax in the future have occurred at the balance sheet date.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>A net deferred tax asset is regarded as\nrecoverable and therefore recognised only when, on the basis of all available\nevidence, it can be regarded as more likely than not that there will be\nsuitable taxable profits from which the future reversal of the underlying\ntiming differences can be deducted.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:&#xD;&#xA;-23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Deferred\ntax is not recognised when fixed assets are revalued unless by the balance\nsheet date there is a binding agreement to sell the revalued assets and the\ngain or loss expected to arise on sale has been recognised in the financial\nstatements.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:&#xD;&#xA;-23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Deferred\ntax is measured on a discounted basis to reflect the time value of money over\nthe period between the balance sheet date and the dates on which it is\nestimated that the timing differences will reverse, or where the timing\ndifferences are not expected to reverse, a period not exceeding 50 years.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>Discount rates of 0.2% to 2.3% have been\nadopted reflecting the post-tax yield to maturity that can be obtained on\ngovernment bonds with similar maturity dates and currencies to those of the\ndeferred tax assets or liabilities.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:&#xD;&#xA;23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><a></a><b><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">2.</span></b><a></a><span style=\"font-size:&#xD;&#xA;11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:&#xD;&#xA;1\">     </span><b>OPERATING PROFIT</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:&#xD;&#xA;-23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>None\nof the directors received any emoluments in respect of their services to the<a></a> company during the year or the prior year.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:&#xD;&#xA;23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span prior year.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align:justify;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-left:23.2pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:&#xD;&#xA;-23.2pt;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span the audit of the company has been borne<a></a> by another group undertaking.</span></p></div><div><span
